//---------------------------------------
// Sound for Armors and Shields
//---------------------------------------
//Definition ingame	|	File Name

//Chat Functions
misc/chat				RMCHAT1		// Doom 2 chat sound
misc/chat2				RMCHAT2		// Chat sound for everything else

//Main Menu
menu/activate			RMACTIVA	// Activate a new menu (Switch sound)
menu/backup				RMBACKUP	// Backup to previous menu (Switch sound)
menu/prompt				RMPROMPT	// Activate a prompt "menu" (switch sound)
menu/cursor				RMCURSOR	// Move cursor up/down (liftend sound)
menu/change				RMCHANGE	// Select new value for option (wallmove sound)
menu/invalid			RMINVALI	// Menu not available (playeruffsound)
menu/dismiss			RMDISMIS	// Dismiss a prompt message (other switchs ound)
menu/choose				RMCHOOSE	// Choose a menu item (pistolfire)
menu/clear				RMCLEAR		// Close top menu (other siwtch sound)

//Quiting the game
menu/gamequit1			RMQUIT1
menu/gamequit2			RMQUIT2
menu/gamequit3			RMQUIT3
$random menu/quit1 { menu/gamequit1 menu/gamequit2 menu/gamequit3 }
$random menu/quit2 { menu/gamequit1 menu/gamequit2 menu/gamequit3 }
